# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="6b773-102">Tipos obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b773-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="6b773-103">As tabelas deste artigo listam os tipos que estão obsoletos no [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] e no [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organizados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b773-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6b773-104">Use os links a seguir para ver uma lista dos tipos obsoletos e das alternativas recomendadas em cada assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b773-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6b773-105">Como esses tipos são obsoletos, todos seus membros também estão obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b773-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6b773-106">Para obter uma lista de membros obsoletos adicionais na biblioteca de classes .NET Framework, confira [Membros obsoletos](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b773-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
